<h2 class="gb-699c267fb5eb8 wp-block-heading is-style-script-text has-text-color has-raleway-font-family" style="color:#f16b7d;font-size:50px;font-style:normal;font-weight:600">Hi! I&#8217;m Michelle.</h2>


<style>@media only screen and (max-width: 600px) {.gb-699c267fba61c{font-size: 18px!important;}}</style>
<p class="gb-699c267fba61c has-poppins-font-family" style="font-size:28px;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">Hey there! I&#8217;m Michelle Moncrief, the friendly face behind Makers Corner Crafts. I live in North Texas with my wonderful husband and our adorable rescue pup, Toby.</p>


<style>@media only screen and (max-width: 600px) {.gb-699c267fbee1b{font-size: 18px!important;}}</style>
<p class="gb-699c267fbee1b has-poppins-font-family" style="font-size:28px;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">At Makers Corner Crafts, I help you tackle those tricky cutting machines and design software with clear, straightforward guidance. </p>


<style>@media only screen and (max-width: 600px) {.gb-699c267fc32d9{font-size: 18px!important;}}</style>
<p class="gb-699c267fc32d9 has-poppins-font-family" style="font-size:28px;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">If technology sometimes feels overwhelming, you&#8217;re in the right place—our supportive community of crafters and growing library of educational resources are designed to help you create with confidence, no matter your tech comfort level.</p>
